<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The fastest way to build AI applications that never go down</h2><a id="user-content-the-fastest-way-to-build-ai-applications-that-never-go-down" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The fastest way to build AI applications that never go down" href="#the-fastest-way-to-build-ai-applications-that-never-go-down"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Bifrost is a high-performance AI gateway that unifies access to 23+ providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, AWS Bedrock, Google Vertex, and more) through a single OpenAI-compatible API. Deploy in seconds with zero configuration and get automatic failover, load balancing, semantic caching, and enterprise-grade features.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/maximhq/bifrost/blob/dev/docs/media/getting-started.png"><img src="/maximhq/bifrost/raw/dev/docs/media/getting-started.png" alt="Get started" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Go from zero to production-ready AI gateway in under a minute.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 1:</strong> Start Bifrost Gateway</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Install and run locally
npx -y @maximhq/bifrost

# Or use Docker
docker run -p 8080:8080 maximhq/bifrost"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install and run locally</span>
npx -y @maximhq/bifrost

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Or use Docker</span>
docker run -p 8080:8080 maximhq/bifrost</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 2:</strong> Configure via Web UI</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Open the built-in web interface
open http://localhost:8080"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Open the built-in web interface</span>
open http://localhost:8080</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Step 3:</strong> Make your first API call</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -X POST http://localhost:8080/v1/chat/completions \
  -H &quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot; \
  -d '{
    &quot;model&quot;: &quot;openai/gpt-4o-mini&quot;,
    &quot;messages&quot;: [{&quot;role&quot;: &quot;user&quot;, &quot;content&quot;: &quot;Hello, Bifrost!&quot;}]
  }'"><pre>curl -X POST http://localhost:8080/v1/chat/completions \
  -H <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Content-Type: application/json<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
  -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "model": "openai/gpt-4o-mini",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": "Hello, Bifrost!"}]</span>
<span class="pl-s">  }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>That's it!</strong> Your AI gateway is running with a web interface for visual configuration, real-time monitoring, and analytics.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Complete Setup Guides:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/gateway/setting-up" rel="nofollow">Gateway Setup</a> - HTTP API deployment</li>
<li><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/go-sdk/setting-up" rel="nofollow">Go SDK Setup</a> - Direct integration</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Enterprise Deployments</h2><a id="user-content-enterprise-deployments" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Enterprise Deployments" href="#enterprise-deployments"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Bifrost supports enterprise-grade, private deployments for teams running production AI systems at scale.
In addition to private networking, custom security controls, and governance, enterprise deployments unlock advanced capabilities including adaptive load balancing, clustering, guardrails, MCP gateway and and other features designed for enterprise-grade scale and reliability.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Features</h2><a id="user-content-key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Features" href="#key-features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Infrastructure</h3><a id="user-content-core-infrastructure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Infrastructure" href="#core-infrastructure"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/providers/supported-providers/overview" rel="nofollow">Unified Interface</a></strong> - Single OpenAI-compatible API for all providers</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/gateway/provider-configuration" rel="nofollow">Multi-Provider Support</a></strong> - OpenAI, Anthropic, AWS Bedrock, Google Vertex, Azure, Cerebras, Cohere, Mistral, Ollama, Groq, and more</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/retries-and-fallbacks" rel="nofollow">Automatic Fallbacks</a></strong> - Seamless failover between providers and models with zero downtime</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/retries-and-fallbacks" rel="nofollow">Load Balancing</a></strong> - Intelligent request distribution across multiple API keys and providers</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Features</h3><a id="user-content-advanced-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Features" href="#advanced-features"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/mcp/overview" rel="nofollow">Model Context Protocol (MCP)</a></strong> - Enable AI models to use external tools (filesystem, web search, databases)</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/semantic-caching" rel="nofollow">Semantic Caching</a></strong> - Intelligent response caching based on semantic similarity to reduce costs and latency</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/gateway/streaming" rel="nofollow">Multimodal Support</a></strong> - Support for text,images, audio, and streaming, all behind a common interface.</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/enterprise/custom-plugins" rel="nofollow">Custom Plugins</a></strong> - Extensible middleware architecture for analytics, monitoring, and custom logic</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/governance/virtual-keys" rel="nofollow">Governance</a></strong> - Usage tracking, rate limiting, and fine-grained access control</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Enterprise &amp; Security</h3><a id="user-content-enterprise--security" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Enterprise &amp; Security" href="#enterprise--security"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/governance/budget-and-limits" rel="nofollow">Budget Management</a></strong> - Hierarchical cost control with virtual keys, teams, and customer budgets</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/enterprise/user-provisioning" rel="nofollow">User Provisioning (OIDC)</a></strong> - OAuth 2.0 / OIDC login with background directory sync for teams, roles, and business units</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/observability/default" rel="nofollow">Observability</a></strong> - Native Prometheus metrics, distributed tracing, and comprehensive logging</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/deployment-guides/config-json#environment-variable-references" rel="nofollow">Secrets Management</a></strong> - Secure API key management with environment variables and deployment secrets</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Developer Experience</h3><a id="user-content-developer-experience" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Developer Experience" href="#developer-experience"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/gateway/setting-up" rel="nofollow">Zero-Config Startup</a></strong> - Start immediately with dynamic provider configuration</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/features/drop-in-replacement" rel="nofollow">Drop-in Replacement</a></strong> - Replace OpenAI/Anthropic/GenAI APIs with one line of code</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/integrations/what-is-an-integration" rel="nofollow">SDK Integrations</a></strong> - Native support for popular AI SDKs with zero code changes</li>
<li><strong><a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/gateway/provider-configuration" rel="nofollow">Configuration Flexibility</a></strong> - Web UI, API-driven, or file-based configuration options</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Repository Structure</h2><a id="user-content-repository-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Repository Structure" href="#repository-structure"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Bifrost uses a modular architecture for maximum flexibility:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bifrost/
├── npx/                 # NPX script for easy installation
├── core/                # Core functionality and shared components
│   ├── providers/       # Provider-specific implementations (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.)
│   ├── schemas/         # Interfaces and structs used throughout Bifrost
│   └── bifrost.go       # Main Bifrost implementation
├── framework/           # Framework components for data persistence
│   ├── configstore/     # Configuration storages
│   ├── logstore/        # Request logging storages
│   └── vectorstore/     # Vector storages
├── transports/          # HTTP gateway and other interface layers
│   └── bifrost-http/    # HTTP transport implementation
├── ui/                  # Web interface for HTTP gateway
├── plugins/             # Extensible plugin system
│   ├── governance/      # Budget management and access control
│   ├── jsonparser/      # JSON parsing and manipulation utilities
│   ├── logging/         # Request logging and analytics
│   ├── maxim/           # Maxim's observability integration
│   ├── mocker/          # Mock responses for testing and development
│   ├── semanticcache/   # Intelligent response caching
│   └── telemetry/       # Monitoring and observability
├── docs/                # Documentation and guides
└── tests/               # Comprehensive test suites"><pre lang="text" class="notranslate"><code>bifrost/
├── npx/                 # NPX script for easy installation

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Getting Started Options</h2><a id="user-content-getting-started-options" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Getting Started Options" href="#getting-started-options"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Choose the deployment method that fits your needs:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Gateway (HTTP API)</h3><a id="user-content-1-gateway-http-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. <p dir="auto"><strong>Best for:</strong> Language-agnostic integration, microservices, and production deployments</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# NPX - Get started in 30 seconds
npx -y @maximhq/bifrost

# Docker - Production ready
docker run -p 8080:8080 -v $(pwd)/data:/app/data maximhq/bifrost"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> NPX - Get started in 30 seconds</span>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Features:</strong> Web UI, real-time monitoring, multi-provider management, zero-config startup</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Learn More:</strong> <a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/quickstart/gateway/setting-up" rel="nofollow">Gateway Setup Guide</a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Drop-in Replacement</h3><a id="user-content-3-drop-in-replacement" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. <div class="highlight highlight-source-diff notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# OpenAI SDK
- base_url = &quot;https://api.openai.com&quot;

<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance</h2><a id="user-content-performance" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance" href="#performance"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Bifrost adds virtually zero overhead to your AI requests. In sustained 5,000 RPS benchmarks, the gateway added only <strong>11 µs</strong> of overhead per request.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Metric</th>
<th>t3.medium</th>
<th>t3.xlarge</th>
<th>Improvement</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Added latency (Bifrost overhead)</td>
<td>59 µs</td>
<td><strong>11 µs</strong></td>
<td><strong>-81%</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Success rate @ 5k RPS</td>
<td>100%</td>
<td>100%</td>
<td>No failed requests</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Avg. queue wait time</td>
<td>47 µs</td>
<td><strong>1.67 µs</strong></td>
<td><strong>-96%</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Avg. request latency (incl. provider)</td>
<td>2.12 s</td>
<td><strong>1.61 s</strong></td>
<td><strong>-24%</strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Key Performance Highlights:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Perfect Success Rate</strong> - 100% request success rate even at 5k RPS</li>
<li><strong>Minimal Overhead</strong> - Less than 15 µs additional latency per request</li>
<li><strong>Efficient Queuing</strong> - Sub-microsecond average wait times</li>
<li><strong>Fast Key Selection</strong> - ~10 ns to pick weighted API keys</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Complete Benchmarks:</strong> <a href="https://docs.getbifrost.ai/benchmarking/getting-started" rel="nofollow">Performance Analysis</a></p>
